               ### Podfile

               ```ruby
               # Uncomment this line to define a global platform for your project
               platform :ios, '16.0'

               # CocoaPods analytics sends network stats synchronously affecting flutter build latency.
               ENV['COCOAPODS_DISABLE_STATS'] = '1'

               project 'Runner', {
                 'Debug' => :debug,
                 'Release' => :release,
                 'Profile' => :profile,
               }

               def flutter_install_ios_engine
                 setup_dir = File.expand_path(File.join('..', '..', '.dart_tool', 'flutter_tools', 'bin'), __FILE__)
                 if File.exist?(setup_dir)
                   return File.join(setup_dir, 'podhelper.rb')
                 end
                 'Flutter/podhelper.rb'
               end

               # Check if podhelper exists in standard Flutter engine location
               podhelper_path = File.expand_path(File.join('Flutter', 'podhelper.rb'), __dir__)
               if File.exist?(podhelper_path)
                 require podhelper_path
               else
                 # Fallback to absolute path from flutter doctor if possible, 
                 # but relative to the Flutter SDK is usually better. 
                 # For now, let's use the one generated by Flutter in the new ios directory.
                 require_relative 'Flutter/podhelper.rb'
               end

               target 'Runner' do
                 use_frameworks!
                 use_modular_headers!

                 flutter_install_all_ios_pods File.dirname(File.realpath(__FILE__))
                 target 'RunnerTests' do
                   inherit! :search_paths
                 end
               end

               post_install do |installer|
                 installer.pods_project.targets.each do |target|
                   flutter_additional_ios_build_settings(target)
                   target.build_configurations.each do |config|
                     # Fix DT_TOOLCHAIN_DIR bug with GoogleMLKit on newer Xcode versions
                     xcconfig_path = config.base_configuration_reference&.real_path
                     if xcconfig_path && File.exist?(xcconfig_path)
                       xcconfig_content = File.read(xcconfig_path)
                       modified_content = xcconfig_content.gsub('DT_TOOLCHAIN_DIR', 'TOOLCHAIN_DIR')
                       File.write(xcconfig_path, modified_content) if modified_content != xcconfig_content
                     end
                     # Suppress deployment target warnings from pods
                     config.build_settings['IPHONEOS_DEPLOYMENT_TARGET'] = '16.0'
                   end
                 end
               end
               ```
